href='/Writing/178910?labeling=true' target='_blank'>翠楼吟 双调</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: 汉川
-----detail

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　秋，至沔省姊山阳。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='435512303b2743359b31b8a3f7db264e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("435512303b2743359b31b8a3f7db264e");'><span id='435512303b2743359b31b8a3f7db264e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>，32岁</div><div id='435512303b2743359b31b8a3f7db264e' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>返汉阳，寓山阳姊氏，作《浣溪沙》，实为怀合肥人作。（著酒行行满袂风）<div id='poem_178882' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178882' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178882?labeling=true' target='_blank'>浣溪沙<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178882")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178882_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_178882'>予女须家沔之山阳，左白湖，右云梦，春水方生，浸数千里。冬寒沙露，衰草入云。丙午之秋，予与安甥或荡舟采菱，或举火罝兔，或观鱼簺下，山行野吟，自适其适，凭虚怅望，因赋是阕</div><div id='poem_preface_178882_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178882'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178882'>著酒行行满袂风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178882'>草枯霜鹘落晴空。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178882'>销魂都在夕阳中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178882_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178882'>恨入<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_178882", 178882, id='poem_sentence_4_178882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_178882'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(178882)'>评注</a><span id='poem_title_178639' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178639?labeling=true' target='_blank'>以“长歌意无极，好为老夫听”为韵奉别沔鄂亲友十首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span id='poem_sentence_1_178639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178639'>念当去石友，烟席凌江湘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178641_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178641'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178641'>英英白龙孙<span class='inlineComment2'>（郑仁举次皋。）</span>，眉目古人气。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178641'>拮据营数椽，下帘草生砌。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178641'>文章作径庭，功用见造次。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178641'>无庸垂罄嗟，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_178641", 178641, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>遗安</span>鹿门意。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178641'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_178641_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_178642' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178642' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178642?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178642_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178642'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178642'>诗人辛国士<span class='inlineComment2'>（辛泌克清。）</span>，句法似阿驹。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178642'>别墅沧浪曲，绿阴禽鸟呼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178642'>颇参金粟眼，渐造文字无。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178642'>儿辈例学语，屋壁祝蒲卢。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178642'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_178642_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_178643' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178643' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178643?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178643_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178643'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178643'>山阴千载人，挥洒照八极。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178643'>只今定武刻，犹带龙虎笔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178643'>单侯出机杼<span class='inlineComment2'>（单炜炳文。）</span>，岂是剑舞得。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178643'>馀波入竹石，绝叹咄咄逼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178643'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_178643_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_178644' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178644' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178644?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178644_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178644'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178644'>异时之罘君，在涅守白颢。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178644'>黄钟欠牛铎，淋漓吊遗稿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178644'>有子殊可人<span class='inlineComment2'>（蔡迨坚吾子字武伯。）</span>，特未见此老。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178644'>客来请论文，但道曲肱好。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178644'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_178644_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_178645' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178645' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178645?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178645_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178645'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178645'>中郎游千霜，曲高复谁为。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178645'>庞翁趣无弦，郑伯功斲鼻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178645'>春风桃花溪，寒渌绕苍翠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178645'>何当从两君，放浪计幽事。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178645'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_178645_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_178646' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178646' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_178646_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178646'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178646'>宦达羞故妻，贫贱厌丘嫂。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178646'>上书云雨迥，还舍笋蕨老。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178646_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178647'>伐木响虚牝，吾愿友褐夫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178647'>九关呀虎豹，何时内高袪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178647'>黄鹄眇云树，鹦鹉澹烟芜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178647'>倚杖得清赏，洗心观本初。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178647_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178647'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_178647_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_178648' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178648' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178648?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178648_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178648'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178648'>孤鸿度关山，风霜催翅翎。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178648'>影低白云暮，哀噭那忍听。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178648'>士生有如此，储粟不满瓶。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178648'>著书穷愁滨，可续离骚经。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178648_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178648'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_178648_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>发汉阳，作《探春慢》别郑次皋诸人，自此不复返鄂。（衰草愁烟）<div id='poem_178892' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178892' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178892?labeling=true' target='_blank'>探春慢</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178892")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178892_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_178892'>予自孩幼从先人宦于古沔，女须因嫁焉。中去复来几二十年，岂惟姊弟之爱，沔之父老儿女子亦莫不予爱也。丙午冬，千岩老人约予过苕霅①，岁晚乘涛载雪而下，顾念依依，殆不能去。作此曲别郑次皋、辛克清、姚刚中诸君。</div><div id='poem_preface_178892_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178892'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178892'>衰草愁烟，乱鸦送日，风沙回旋平野。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178892_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178892'>拂雪金鞭，欺寒茸帽，还记章台走马。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178892_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178892'>谁念漂零久，漫赢得幽怀难写。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178892_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178892'>故人清沔相逢，小窗闲共情话。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178892_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178892'>长恨离多会少，重访问竹西，珠泪盈把。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178892_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178892'>雁碛波平，渔汀人散，老去不堪游冶。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178892_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178892'>无奈苕溪月，又照我扁舟东下。<div id='poem_sentence_6_178892_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178892'>甚日归来，梅花零乱春夜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_178892_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_178892'><a href='javascript: 扬州

<div class='label1' id='5d68ea5a60cf459a86ab27a4c55fa35a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5d68ea5a60cf459a86ab27a4c55fa35a");'><span id='5d68ea5a60cf459a86ab27a4c55fa35a_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　至日，过维扬，作《扬州慢》（淮左名都）<div id='poem_178856' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178856' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178856?labeling=true' target='_blank'>扬州慢（中吕宫）</a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_preface_178856'>淳熙丙申至日，予过维扬。夜雪初霁，荠麦弥望。入其城，则四顾萧条，寒水自碧，暮色渐起，戍角悲吟。予怀怆然，感慨今昔，因自度此曲。千岩老人以为有《黍离》之悲也</div><div id='poem_preface_178856_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_178856", 178856, "Clauses/2/Comments/1")'>初程</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178856_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178856_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178856'>杜郎<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_178856", 178856, -----title
常德

庐江
-----detail

长沙

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年1月7日</a>　人日，客长沙别驾之观正堂，乱湘流入麓山，作《一萼红》（古城阴）<div id='poem_178828' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178828' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178828?labeling=true' target='_blank'>一萼红</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年1月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_178897'>长溪杨声后典长沙楫棹，居濒湘江。窗间所见，如燕公郭熙画图，卧起幽适。丙午七月既望，声伯约予与赵景鲁、景望、萧和父、裕父、时父、恭父大舟浮湘，放乎中流。山水空寒，烟月交映，凄然其为秋也。坐客皆小冠綀服，或弹琴、或浩歌、或自酌、或援笔搜句。予度此曲，即念奴娇之鬲指声也，于双调中吹之。鬲指亦谓之过腔，见晁无咎集。凡能吹竹者，便能过腔也</div><div id='poem_sentence_0_178829'>芳莲坠粉，疏桐吹绿，庭院暗雨乍歇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178829_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178829'>无端抱影销魂处，还见筱<sup class='reference id='poem_sentence_4_178829'>长恨相从未款，而今何事，又对西风离别。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178829_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178829'>渚寒烟淡，棹移人远，缥缈行舟如叶。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178829_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178829'>想文君望久，倚竹愁生步罗袜。<div id='poem_sentence_6_178829_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178829'>归来后，翠尊<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_178829", 178829, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>双饮</span>，下了珠帘，玲珑闲看月。</div><div id='poem_title_178915' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178915?labeling=true' target='_blank'>霓裳中序第一</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178915")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178915_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_178915'>丙午岁，留长沙，登祝融，因得其祠神之曲曰黄帝盐、苏合香。又于乐工故书中得商调霓裳曲十八阕，皆虚谱无辞。按沈氏乐律，霓裳道调，此乃商调。乐天诗云：“散序六阕”，此特两阕，未知孰是。然音书闲雅，不类今曲。予不暇尽作，作中序一阕传于世。予方羁游，感此古音，不自知其辞之怨抑也</div><div id='poem_preface_178915_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178915'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178915'>亭皋正望极。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178915'>多病却无气力。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178915'>况纨扇渐疏，罗衣初索。<div href='/Writing/474634?labeling=true' target='_blank'>醉吟商小品</a><span class='authorDate'>（1191年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>掇送</span>刘郎老。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178873_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178873'>淮南好。<div id='poem_sentence_6_178873'>陌上生春草。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_178873_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_178873'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(178873)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='20a1682fe9a44bd395d1990c25a3c7d5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("20a1682fe9a44bd395d1990c25a3c7d5");'><span id='20a1682fe9a44bd395d1990c25a3c7d5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>，33岁</div><div id='20a1682fe9a44bd395d1990c25a3c7d5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　三月后，游杭州，以萧徳藻介，袖诗谒杨万里，万里许其文似陆龟蒙，并以诗送往见范成大。作《次韵诚斋送仆往见石湖长句》<div id='poem_178693' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178693' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178693?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵诚斋送仆往见石湖长句</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178693")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178693_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178693'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178693'>客来读赋作雌蜺，平生未闻衡说诗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178693'>省中诗人官事了，狎鸥入梦心无机。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178693'>韵高落落悬清月，铿锵妙语春冰裂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178693'>一自长安识子云，三叹郢中无白雪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178693'>范公萧爽思出尘，有客如此渠不贫。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178693'>堂堂五字作城守，平章劲敌君在口。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178693'>二公句法妙万夫，西来囊中藏鲁玙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_178693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178693'>只今击节乌栖曲，不愧当年贺鉴湖。<div id='poem_sentence_7_178693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_178693'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_178693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_178693'><span class='label'>附杨万里原玉：</span>送姜尧章谒石湖先生<br />钓璜英气横白蜺，咳唾珠玉皆新诗。江山愁诉莺为泣，鬼神露索天泄机。彭蠡波心弄明月，诗星入肠肺肝裂。吐作春风百种花，吹散濒湖数峰雪。青鞋布袜软红尘，千诗只博一字贫。吾友彝陵萧太守，逢人说项不离口。袖诗东来谒老夫，惭无高价索璠玙。翻然欲买松江艇，径去苏州参石湖。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_178693_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='3f3de7f2bbb14ed48b4afe58a5bb6e77_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3f3de7f2bbb14ed48b4afe58a5bb6e77");'><span id='3f3de7f2bbb14ed48b4afe58a5bb6e77_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年</a>　客临安。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d9ace1a73cc44207bd9fed3c5d6fae8e_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>，35岁</div><div id='d9ace1a73cc44207bd9fed3c5d6fae8e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　往来临安，游西湖，作《念奴娇》（闹红一舸）<div id='poem_178869' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178869' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178869?labeling=true' target='_blank'>念奴娇<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178869")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178869_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_178869'>予客武陵，湖北极宪治在焉。古城野水，乔木参天。予与二三友日荡舟其间，薄荷花而饮。意象幽闲，不类人境。秋水且涸，荷叶出地寻丈，因列坐其下。上不见日，清风徐来，绿云自动。间于疏处窥见游人画船，亦一乐也。朅来吴兴，数得相羊荷花中。又夜泛西湖，光景奇绝。故以此句写之</div><div id='poem_preface_178869_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178869'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178869'>闹红一舸，记来时、尝与鸳鸯为侣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178869_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178869'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_178869", 178869, id='poem_sentence_1_178869_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178869'>翠叶吹凉，玉容销酒，更洒菰蒲雨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178869_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178869'>嫣然摇动，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_178869", 178869, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>冷香</span>飞上诗句。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178869_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178869'>日暮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_178869", 178869, id='poem_title_178666_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_178666'>通仲与诚斋为乡人，近来赴调，而诚斋去国。又通仲久与千岩有苕霅之约而未至，余挽通仲，欲与同归千岩，故末章及之。</div><div id='poem_preface_178666_comment'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_178666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_178666'>示疾不下堂，有句高八米。<div id='poem_sentence_9_178666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' gray;'>▪</span>春，与张鉴自越之杭，携家妓观梅于孤山之西村，作《莺声绕红楼》（十亩梅花作雪飞）<div id='poem_178888' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178888' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178888?labeling=true' target='_blank'>莺声绕红楼 甲辰春，平甫与予自越来吴，携家妓观梅于孤山之西村，命国工吹笛，妓皆以柳黄为衣</a><span class='authorDate'>（1194年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178888")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178888_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178888'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178888'>十亩梅花作雪飞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178888_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178888_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178888'>长笛为予吹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178888_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178888_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178888'>近前舞丝丝。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_178888_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>与俞灏燕游西湖，观梅于孤山之西村。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>俞商卿归吴兴，姜夔独游孤山，作《角招》（为春瘦）<div id='poem_178864' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178864' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178864?labeling=true' target='_blank'>角招（黄钟角）</a><span class='authorDate'>（1194年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178864")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178864_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_178864'>甲寅春，予与俞商卿燕游西湖，观梅于孤山之西村。玉雪照映，吹香薄人。已而商卿归吴兴，予独来，则山横春烟，新柳被水，游人容与飞花中。怅然有怀，作此寄之。商卿善歌声，稍以儒雅缘饰。予每自度曲，吟洞箫，商卿辄歌而和之，极有山林缥缈之思。今予离忧，商卿一行作吏，殆无复此乐矣</div><div id='poem_preface_178864_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178864'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178864'>为春瘦。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178864'>何堪更绕西湖，尽是垂柳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178864'>自看烟外岫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178864'>记得与君，湖上携手。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178864'>君归未久。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178864'>犹有。<div id='poem_sentence_7_178864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_178864'>画船<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_178864", 178864, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>障袖</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_178864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_178864'>青楼倚扇，相映人争秀。<div id='poem_sentence_9_178864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_178864", 178864, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>宫黄</span>，而今时候。<div id='poem_sentence_11_178864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178689'>向来相闻不相值，长安城中乃相识。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178689'>如君笔墨与性合，妙处特过苏李前。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178689'>我如切切秋虫语，自诡平生用心苦。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178689'>神凝或与元气接，屡举似君君亦许。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年3月</a>　张鉴欲治舟往武康任职，恐同游不可再，作《鹧鸪天》（曾共君侯历聘来）<div id='poem_178920' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178920' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178920?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鹧鸪天<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1196年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178920")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178920_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_178920'>予与张平甫自南昌同游西山玉隆宫，止宿而返，盖乙卯三月十四日也。是日即平甫初度，因买酒茅舍，并坐古枫下。古枫，旌阳在时物也。旌阳尝以草屦悬其上，土人谓屦为屐，因名曰挂屐枫。苍山四围，平野尽绿，隔涧野花红白，照影可喜，使人采撷，以藤纠缠著枫上。少焉月出，大于黄金盆。逸兴横生，遂成痛饮，午夜乃寝。明年，平甫初度，欲治舟往封禺松竹间，念此游之不可再也，歌以寿之</div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年</a>　秋，与张鎡会饮张达可家，作《齐天乐》蟋蟀词。（庾郎先自吟愁赋）<div id='poem_178861' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178861' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178861?labeling=true' target='_blank'>齐天乐</a><span class='authorDate'>（1196年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_preface_178861'>丙辰岁，与张功父会饮张达可之堂。闻屋壁间蟋蟀有声，功父约予同赋，以授歌者。功父先成，辞甚美。予裴徊末利花间，仰见秋月，顿起幽思，寻亦得此。蟋蟀，中都呼为促织，善斗。好事者或以二三十万钱致一枚，镂象齿为楼观以贮之。</div><div id='poem_preface_178861_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178861'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178861'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_178861", 178861, ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年</a>　既归，录所得诗若干解为一卷，名之曰《载雪录》<br /><a href="javascript: href='/Writing/178910?labeling=true' target='_blank'>翠楼吟 双调</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_preface_178910'>淳熙丙午冬，武昌安远楼成，与刘去非诸友落之，度曲见志。予去武昌十年，故人有泊舟鹦鹉洲者，闻小姬歌此词，问之颇能道其事，还吴为予言之。兴怀昔游，且伤今之离索也</div><div id='poem_preface_178910_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1197&endYear=1197')">1197年</a>　秋，在杭州，作丁巳七月望湖上书事。<div id='poem_178686' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178686' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_4_178713_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1198&endYear=1198')">1198年</a>　作戊午春帖子。<div id='poem_178787' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178787' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178787?labeling=true' target='_blank'>戊午春帖子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1198年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178787")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_178787_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178787'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178787'>晴窗日日拟雕虫，惆怅明时不易逢。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178787_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178787'>二十五弦人不识，淡黄杨柳舞春风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178787_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178787'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_178787_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1199')">1199年</a>　上圣宋铙歌鼓吹十二章。<div id='poem_1288454' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1288454' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1288454?labeling=true' target='_blank'>作鼓吹曲以歌祖宗功德议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1199年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_1288454")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1288454_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1288454'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1288454'>古者，祖宗有功德，必有诗歌，七月之陈王业是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1288454_comment'></div>歌于军中，周之恺乐、恺歌是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1288454_comment'></div>汉有短箫铙歌之曲，凡二十二篇，军中谓之骑吹，其曲曰《战城南》、《圣人出》之类是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1288454_comment'></div>魏因其声，制为《克官渡》等曲十有二篇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1288454_comment'></div>晋亦制为《征辽东》等曲二十篇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1288454_comment'></div>唐柳宗元亦尝作为铙歌十有二篇，述高祖、太宗功烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1288454_comment'></div>我朝太祖、太宗平僭伪，一区宇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1288454_comment'></div>真宗一戎衣而却契丹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1288454_comment'></div>仁宗海涵春育，德如尧、舜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1288454_comment'></div>高宗再造大功，上俪祖宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1288454_comment'></div>愿诏文学之臣，追述功业之盛，作为歌诗，使知乐者协以音律，领之太常，以播于天下。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1288454_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1199')">1199年</a>　诏免解。与试礼部，不第。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1199')">1199年</a>　秋，与韩淲、潘柽、蓋希之游西林看木樨。<br id='poem_sentence_0_178747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178747'>平生最识江湖味，听得秋声忆故乡。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href='/Writing/178895?labeling=true' target='_blank'>喜迁莺慢/喜迁莺 太簇宫功父新第落成</a><span class='authorDate'>（1200年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>朱组</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178895'>又占了、道人林下真趣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178895'>总付与、在柳桥花馆，玲珑深处。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178895'>居士。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178895'>闲记取。<div id='poem_sentence_6_178895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178895'>高卧未成，且种松千树。<div id='poem_sentence_7_178895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_178895'>觅句堂深，写经窗静，他日任听风雨。<div id='poem_sentence_8_178895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_178895'>列仙更教谁做，一院双成俦侣。<div id='poem_sentence_9_178895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_178895'>世间住。<div id='poem_sentence_10_178895_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_178895'>且休将鸡犬，云中飞去。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_178895_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1201&endYear=1201')">1201年</a>　《昔游诗》当作于此年。作品：昔游诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈思认为《昔游诗》作于庆元三年（1197），《白石年谱》第2145页。）</span><div id='poem_178668' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178668' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178668?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昔游诗十五首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1201年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178668")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178668_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_178668'>夔蚤岁孤贫，奔走川陆，数年以来，始获宁处。秋日无谓，追述旧游，可喜可愕者，吟为五字古句。时欲展阅自省，生平不足以为诗也。</div><div id='poem_preface_178668_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178668'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178668'>洞庭八百里，玉盘盛水银。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178668_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178668'>长虹忽照影，大哉五色轮。<div id='poem_sentence_8_178676_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_178676'>古杉晋时物，中空野人住。<div id='poem_sentence_9_178676_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_178676'>外围四十尺，内可十客聚。<div id='poem_sentence_10_178676_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_178676'>我游瞿仙馆，坛上表遗步。<div id='poem_sentence_11_178676_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_178676'>却下八叠坡，一亭众妙具。<div id='poem_sentence_12_178676_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_178676'>两山抱澄潭，老木枝干互。<div id='poem_sentence_13_178676_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_178676'>瞻前秀而迥，坐久凛难驻。<div id='poem_sentence_14_178676_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_178676'>桃源独不见，僻在宫南路。<div id='poem_sentence_15_178676_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_178676'>山行转深邃，狙猿纷上下。<div id='poem_sentence_16_178676_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_178676'>石窦出微涓，令我意犹豫。<div id='poem_sentence_17_178676_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_178676'>昔闻渔舟子，水际见洞户。<div id='poem_sentence_18_178676_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_178676'>今看去溪远，定自后人误。<div id='poem_sentence_19_178676_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_178676'>惆怅却归来，此游不得屡。<div id='poem_sentence_20_178676_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_178676'>于今二十年，历历经行处。<div id='poem_sentence_21_178676_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_178676'></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_178676_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_178677' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178677' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178677?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1201年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178677_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178677'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178677'>昔游衡山下，看水入朱陵<span class='inlineComment2'>（桃源县界。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178677'>半空扫积雪，万万玉花凝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178677'>或如生绡挂，或如薄雾横。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178677'>纷纷虎豹吼，往往蛟龙惊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178677'>人语不相闻，溅雹漂风缨。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178677'>有鱼缘峭壁，上上终不停。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178677'>此中有神物，雷雨周八纮。<div id='poem_sentence_6_178677_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178677'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_178677_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_178678' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178678' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178678?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1201年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178678_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178678'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178678'>昔游衡山上，未晓入幽谷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178678'>欲识所坐舆，横板挂两竹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178678'>状如秋千垂，高下不倾覆。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178678'>登山九千丈，中道多佛屋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178678'>一峰高一峰，峰峰秀林木。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178678'>仰看同来客，木末见冠服。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178678'>高台石桥路，寻常云所宿。<div id='poem_sentence_6_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178678'>下方雷雨时，此上自晴旭。<div id='poem_sentence_7_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_178678'>紫盖何突兀，万里在一目。<div id='poem_sentence_8_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_178678'>馀峰六七十，仅如翠浪矗。<div id='poem_sentence_9_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_178678'>北有懒瓒岩，大石庇樵牧。<div id='poem_sentence_10_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_178678'>下窥半厓花，杯盂琢红玉。<div id='poem_sentence_11_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_178678'>飞云身畔遇，揽之不盈掬。<div id='poem_sentence_12_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_178678'>祝融最高绝，紫盖不足录。<div id='poem_sentence_13_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_178678'>俯视同仰观，苍苍万形伏。<div id='poem_sentence_14_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_178678'>惟馀岣嵝峰，南睇半空绿。<div id='poem_sentence_15_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_178678'>髣髴认潇湘，向岳流屈曲。<div id='poem_sentence_16_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_178678'>高处惊我魂，翻思宅平陆。<div id='poem_sentence_17_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_178678'>其东有雷穴，灵异谨勿触。<div id='poem_sentence_18_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_178678'>云来绵世界，云去一峰独。<div id='poem_sentence_19_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_178678'>僧窗或留罅，云入不可逐。<div id='poem_sentence_20_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_178678'>绝顶横石梁，仙人有遗躅。<div id='poem_sentence_21_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_178678'>山多金光草，夜半如列烛。<div id='poem_sentence_22_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_178678'>灵药不可寻，吁嗟归太速。<div id='poem_sentence_23_178678_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_178678'></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_178678_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_178679' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178679' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_178679_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178679'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178679'>濠梁四无山，坡陁亘长野。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178679'>吾披紫茸毡，纵饮面无赭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178679'>自矜意气豪，敢骑雪中马。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178679'>行行逆风去，初亦略沾洒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178679'>疾风吹大片，忽若乱飘瓦。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178679'>侧身当其冲，丝鞚袖中把。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178679'>重围万箭急，驰突更叱咤。<div id='poem_sentence_6_178679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178679'>酒力不支吾，数里进一斝。<div id='poem_sentence_7_178679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_178679'>燎茅烘湿衣，客有见留者。<div id='poem_sentence_8_178679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_178679'>徘徊望神州，沈叹英雄寡。<div id='poem_sentence_9_178679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_178679'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_178679_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_178680' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178680' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178680?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1201年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178680_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178680'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178680'>既离湖口县，未至落星湾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178680'>舟中两三程，程程见庐山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178680'>庐山遮半天，五老云为冠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178680'>朝看金叠叠，暮看紫巉巉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178680'>瀑布在山半，髣髴认一斑。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178680'>庐山忽不见，云雨满人间。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178680'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_178680_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_178681' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178681' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_178681_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178681'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178681'>雪霁下扬子，閒望江上山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178681'>山山如白玉，日照金孱颜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178681'>是时江水净，影落清镜寒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178681'>潮催庾信老，云送佛狸还。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178681'>万古感心事，惆怅垂杨湾。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178681'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_178681_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_178682' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178682' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178682?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1201年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178682_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178682'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178682'>衡山为真宫，道士饮我酒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178682'>共坐有何人，山中白衣叟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178682'>问叟家何在，近住山洞口。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178682'>殷勤起见邀，徐步入林薮。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178682'>云深险径黑，石乱湍水吼。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178682'>寻源行渐远，茅屋剪如帚。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178682'>老烹茶味苦，野琢琴形丑。<div id='poem_sentence_6_178682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178682'>叟云司马迁，学道此居久。<div id='poem_sentence_7_178682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_178682'>屋东大磐石，棋画今尚有。<div id='poem_sentence_8_178682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_178682'>古木庇覆之，清泉石根走。<div id='poem_sentence_9_178682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_178682'>因悲百年内，汲汲成白首。<div id='poem_sentence_10_178682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_178682'>仙人固难值，隐者亦可偶。<div id='poem_sentence_11_178682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_178682'>追惟恍如梦，欲画无好手。<div id='poem_sentence_12_178682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_178682'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_178682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_178682'><span class='label'>附：</span>书昔游诗后　　潘柽<br /> 　　我行半天下，未能到潇湘。君诗如画图，历历记所尝。起我远游兴，其如鬓毛霜。何以舒此怀，转轸弹清商。<br /> 　　又　　韩淲<br /> 　　平生未踏洞庭野，亦不曾登南岳峰。因君谈旧游，恍如常相从。江淮历历转湘浦，裘马意气传边烽。吾尝汎大江，只见匡庐松。乘风醉卧帆影底，高浪直溅岚光浓。日暮泊船时，是夜方严冬。雪花压船船背重，缆摇柂鼓声如钟。当年意浅语不到，无句可写波涛舂。君诗乃如许，景物不易供。尽归一毫端，状□□□□。人间胜处贵著眼，虽有此兴无由逢。钱唐山水亦自好，奈何薄宦难从容。南高北高一千丈，潮头日夜鸣灵踪。应有隐者为识赏，青鞋布袜扶杖筇。君无诧彼我愧此，急还诗卷心徒忪。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_178682_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='6aeecf707169404ebb04175860c583ca_label'><a href='javascript: id='poem_sentence_2_178816_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_178817' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178817' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178817?labeling=true' -----title
湖州
-----detail

id='poem_preface_178890'>吴兴号水晶宫，荷花盛丽。陈简斋云：“今年何以报君恩。一路荷花相送到青墩。”亦可见矣。丁未之夏，予游千岩，数往来红香中。自度此曲，以无射宫歌之</div><div id='poem_preface_178890_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178890'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178890'>簟枕邀凉，琴书换日，睡馀无力。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178890_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178890'>细洒冰泉，并刀破甘碧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178737'>但得明年少行役，只裁白纻作春衫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178737_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178737'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_178737_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_178738' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178738' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_178738_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178738'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178738'>少小知名翰墨场，十年心事只凄凉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178738_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178738'>旧时曾作梅花赋，研墨于今亦自香。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178738_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178738'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_178738_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_178739' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178739' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_178739_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178739'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178739'>环玦随波冷未销，古苔留雪卧墙腰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178739_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178739'>谁家玉笛吹春怨，看见鹅黄上柳条。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178739_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年</a>　大雪过垂虹桥，作诗。<div id='poem_178766' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178766' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178766?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过垂虹</a><span class='authorDate'>（1191年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>小红</span>低唱我吹箫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178766_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178766'>曲终过尽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_178766", 178766, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>松陵</span>路，回首烟波十四桥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178766_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
苏州
-----detail

class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_178852", 178852, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>三高</span>，游衍佳处。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178852_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178852_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178852'>浮云安在，我自爱、绿香红舞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178852_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178852'>见说胡儿，也学纶巾攲雨。<div id='poem_sentence_7_178852_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_178852'>玉友金蕉，玉人金缕。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178741_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='f4a459f3616a401bb18a70714e761591_label'><a href='javascript: gray;'>▪</span>载雪谒范成大于苏州，作《雪中访石湖》诗，石湖有和。<div id='poem_178663' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178663' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178663?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雪中访石湖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1191年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178663")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178663_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178663'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178663'>雪矸如玉城，偏师敢轻犯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178663'>黄芦阵野鹜，我自将十万。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178663'>三战渠未降，北面石湖范。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178663'>先生霸越手，定自一笑粲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178663'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_178663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_178663'><span class='label'>附范成大和诗：</span>次韵尧章雪中见赠<br />玉龙阵长空，皋比忽先犯。鳞甲塞天飞，战退三百万。当时访戴舟，却访一寒范。新诗如美人，蓬荜愧三粲。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_178663_comment'></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>赏梅范村，作《玉梅令》（疏疏雪片）<div id='poem_178851' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178851' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178851?labeling=true' target='_blank'>玉梅令</a><span class='authorDate'>（1191年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178851")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178851_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_178851'>石湖家自制此声，未有语实之，命予作。石湖宅南，隔河有圃曰苑村，梅开雪落，竹院深静，而石湖畏寒不出，故戏及之。</div><div id='poem_preface_178851_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178851'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178851'>疏疏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_178851", 178851, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>雪片</span>，散入溪南苑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178851'>春寒锁、旧家亭馆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178851'>有玉梅几树，背立怨东风，高花未吐，暗香已远。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178851'>公来领客，梅花能劝，花长好、愿公更健。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178851_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178851'>便揉春为酒，剪雪作新诗，拚一日、绕花千转。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_178851_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>范成大征新声，姜夔作《暗香》（旧时月色|）<div id='poem_178917' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178917' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178917?labeling=true' target='_blank'>暗香</a><span class='authorDate'>（1191年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178917")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178917_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_178917'>辛亥之冬，予载雪诣石湖。止既月，授简索句，且征新声，作此两曲。石湖把玩不已，使工妓隶习之，音节谐婉，乃名之曰《暗香》《疏影》。</div><div id='poem_preface_178917_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178917'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178917'>旧时月色，算几番照我，梅边吹笛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178917'>唤起玉人，不管清寒与攀摘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178917'>何逊而今渐老，都忘却春风<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_178917", 178917, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>词笔</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178917'>但怪得竹外疏花，香冷入瑶席。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178917_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178917'>江国，正寂寂。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178917'>叹寄与路遥，夜雪初积。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178917'>翠尊易泣，红萼无言耿相忆。<div id='poem_sentence_6_178917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178917'>长记曾携手处，千树压西湖<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_178917", 178917, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>寒碧</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_178917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_178917'>又片片、吹尽也，几时见得。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_178917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_178917'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(178917)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>范成大征新声，姜夔作《疏影》（苔枝缀玉）<div id='poem_178900' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178900' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178900?labeling=true' target='_blank'>疏影</a><span class='authorDate'>（1191年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178900")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178900_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178900'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178900'>苔枝缀玉，有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_178900", 178900, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>翠禽</span>小小，枝上同宿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178900'>客里相逢，篱角黄昏，无言自倚修竹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178900'>昭君不惯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_178900", 178900, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>胡沙</span>远，但暗忆、江南江北。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178900'>想<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_178900", 178900, "Clauses/8/Comments/1")'>佩环</span>、月夜归来，化作此花幽独。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178900_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178900'>犹记深宫旧事，那人正睡里，飞近<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_178900", 178900, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>蛾绿</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178900'>莫似春风，不管盈盈，早与安排金屋。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178900'>还教一片随波去，又却怨、玉龙哀曲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_178900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178900'>等恁时、重觅幽香，已入小窗横幅。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_178900_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_178900'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年12月</a>　范成大九月卒，十二月姜夔赴苏州悼之，有诗三首。作品：悼石湖（三首）<div id='poem_178700' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178700' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a -----title
合肥

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年7月7日</a>　七夕，在合肥与赵君猷坐月，作《摸鱼儿》（向秋来）<div id='poem_178902' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178902' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_178902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178902'>闲记省。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_178902", 178902, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>银波</span>相望千顷。<div id='poem_sentence_7_178902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_178902'>柳州老矣犹儿戏，瓜果为伊三请。<div id='poem_sentence_8_178902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_178902'>云路迥。<div id='poem_sentence_9_178902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_178902'>漫说道、年年野鹊曾并影。<div id='poem_sentence_10_178902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_178902'>无人与问。<div id='poem_sentence_11_178902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_178902'>但浊酒相呼，疏帘自捲，微月照清饮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_178902_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年</a>　寓合肥，作《凄凉犯》。此时情侣似已离合肥，此后白石诗词无合肥踪迹。（绿杨巷陌秋风起）<div id='poem_178880' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178880' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178880?labeling=true' target='_blank'>凄凉犯（仙吕调犯商调）</a><span class='authorDate'>（1191年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178880")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178880_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_178880'>合肥苍陌皆种柳，秋风夕起骚骚然。予客居阖户，时闻马嘶。出城四顾，则荒烟野草，不胜凄黯，乃著此解。琴有凄凉调，假以为名。凡曲言犯者，谓以宫犯商、商犯宫之类。如道调宫上字住，双调亦上字住。所住字同，故道调曲中犯双调，或于双调曲中犯道调，其他准此。唐人乐书云：犯有正、旁、偏、侧。宫犯宫为正，宫犯商为旁，宫犯角为偏，宫犯羽为侧。此说非也。十二宫所住字各不同，不容相犯，十二宫特可犯商、角、羽耳。予归行都，以此曲示国工田正德，使以哑觱栗角吹之，其韵极美，亦曰瑞鹤仙影</div><div id='poem_preface_178880_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178880'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178880'>绿杨巷陌。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178880'>秋风起、边城一片<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_178880", 178880, "Clauses/1/Comments/1")'>离索</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178880'>马嘶渐远，人归甚处，戍楼吹角。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178880'>情怀正恶。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178880'>更衰草寒烟淡薄。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178880'>似当时、将军部曲，迤逦度沙漠。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178880_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178880'>追念西湖上，小舫携歌，晚花行乐。<div id='poem_sentence_6_178880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178880'>旧游在否，想如今、翠凋红落。<div id='poem_sentence_7_178880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_178880'>漫写<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_178880", 178880, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>羊裙</span>，等新雁来时系著。<div id='poem_sentence_8_178880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_178880'>怕匆匆、不肯寄与，误后约。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_178880_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_178880'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(178880)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年</a>　作《秋宵吟》（古帘空）<div id='poem_178879' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178879' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178879?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋宵吟 越调</a><span class='authorDate'>（1191年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178879")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178879_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178879'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178879'>古帘空，坠月皎。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178879'>坐久西窗人悄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178879'>蛩吟苦，渐漏水丁丁，箭壶催晓。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178879'>引凉飔、动翠葆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178879'>露脚斜飞云表。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178879'>因嗟念，似去国情怀，暮帆烟草。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178879_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178879'>带眼销磨，为近日、愁多顿老。<div id='poem_sentence_6_178879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178879'>卫娘何在，宋玉归来，两地暗萦绕。<div id='poem_sentence_7_178879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_178879'>摇落江枫早。<div id='poem_sentence_8_178879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_178879'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_178879", 178879, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>嫩约</span>无凭，幽梦又杳。<div id='poem_sentence_9_178879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_178879'>但盈盈、泪洒单衣，今夕何夕恨未了。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_178879_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年</a>　别合肥，作《解连环》（玉鞭重倚）<div id='poem_178909' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178909' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178909?labeling=true' target='_blank'>解连环</a><span class='authorDate'>（1191年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178909")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178909_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178909'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178909'>玉鞭重倚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178909'>却沈吟未上，又萦离思。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178909'>为大乔、能拨春风，小乔妙<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_178909", 178909, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>移筝</span>，雁啼秋水。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178909'>柳怯云松，更何必、十分梳洗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178909'>道郎携羽扇，那日隔帘，半面曾记。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178909_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178909'>西窗夜凉雨霁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178909'>叹幽欢未足，何事轻弃。<div id='poem_sentence_6_178909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178909'>问后约、空指蔷薇，算如此溪山，甚时重至。<div id='poem_sentence_7_178909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_178909'>水驿灯昏，又见在、曲屏近底。<div id='poem_sentence_8_178909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_178909'>念唯有、夜来皓月，照伊自睡。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_178909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_178909'><a href='javascript: -----title
巢湖
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='79288d83acf24a4e8248243b50596dc8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("79288d83acf24a4e8248243b50596dc8");'><span id='79288d83acf24a4e8248243b50596dc8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年</a>，37岁</div><div id='79288d83acf24a4e8248243b50596dc8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年1月30日</a>　晦日泛巢湖，作平韵《满江红》（仙姥来时）<div id='poem_178903' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178903' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178903?labeling=true' target='_blank'>满江红</a><span class='authorDate'>（1191年1月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178903")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178903_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_178903'>满江红旧调用仄韵，多不协律。如末句云「无心扑」三字，歌者将“心”字融入去声，方协音律。予欲以平韵为之，久不能成。因泛巢湖，闻远岸箫鼓声，问之舟师，云“居人为此湖神姥寿也。”予因祝曰：“得一席风径至居巢，当以平韵满江红为迎送神曲。”言讫，风与笔俱驶，顷刻而成。末句云「闻佩环」，则协律矣。书于绿笺，沉于白浪，辛亥正月晦也。是年六月，复过祠下，因刻之柱间。有客来自居巢云：“土人祠姥，辄能歌此词。”按曹操至濡须口，孙权遗操书曰：“春水方生，公宜速去。”操曰：“孙权不欺孤”，乃撤军还。濡须口与东关相近，江湖水之所出入。予意春水方生，必有司之者，故归其功于姥云。</div><div id='poem_preface_178903_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178903'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178903'>仙姥来时，正一望、千顷翠澜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178903'>旌旗共乱云俱下，依约前山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178903'>命驾群龙金作轭，相从<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_178903", 178903, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>诸娣</span>玉为冠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178903'>向夜深、风定悄无人，闻佩环。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178903_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178903'>神奇处，君试看。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178903'>奠淮右，阻江南。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178903'>遣六丁雷电，别守东关。<div id='poem_sentence_6_178903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178903'>却笑英雄无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_178903", 178903, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>好手</span>，一篙春水走曹瞒。<div id='poem_sentence_7_178903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_178903'>又怎知、人在小红楼，帘影间。<div id='poem_sentence_8_178903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_178903'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_178903_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_178903'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(178903)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='cdfdc4dfe3e54a35bd5ff74f50ba1048_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cdfdc4dfe3e54a35bd5ff74f50ba1048");'><span id='cdfdc4dfe3e54a35bd5ff74f50ba1048_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年</a>，37岁</div><div id='cdfdc4dfe3e54a35bd5ff74f50ba1048' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年6月</a>　复过巢湖，刻平韵《满江红》（仙姥来时）于神姥祠柱间。<br /></div>
-----end

绍兴

id='poem_sentence_0_178780'>秦山越树两依依，閒倚阑干看落晖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178780'>杨柳梢头春又暗，玉箫声里夜游归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178780_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178780'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_178780_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>作诗咏项里苔梅。<div id='poem_178773' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178773' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178773?labeling=true' target='_blank'>项里</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178773")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_178773_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_178773'>项里，项王之里也。在山阴西南二十馀里，地多杨梅苔梅，皆妙天下。王性之赋项里杨梅云：“只今枝头万颗红，犹似咸阳三月火。”予近得苔梅一株，古怪特甚，为作七言。</div><div id='poem_preface_178773_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178773'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178773'>旧国婆娑几树梅，将军逐鹿未归来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178773_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178773'>江东父老空相忆，枝上年年长绿苔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178773_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178773'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_178773_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='8edf71ab14c2488cb9b8161a039b2a6c_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>，39岁</div><div id='8edf71ab14c2488cb9b8161a039b2a6c' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，与黄庆长夜泛鉴湖，作《水龙吟》（夜深客子移舟处）<div id='poem_178844' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178844' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178844?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水龙吟 黄庆长夜泛鉴湖，有怀归之曲，课予和之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178844")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178844_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178844'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178844'>夜深客子移舟处，两两沙禽惊起。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178844'>红衣入桨，青灯摇浪，微凉意思。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178844'>把酒临风，不思归去，有如此水。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178844'>况茂陵游倦，长干望久，芳心事、箫声里。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178844_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178844'>屈指归期尚未。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178844'>鹊南飞、有人应喜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178844'>画阑桂子，留香小待，提携影底。<div id='poem_sentence_6_178844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178844'>我已情多，十年幽梦，略曾如此。<div id='poem_sentence_7_178844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_178844'>甚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_178844", 178844, "Clauses/19/Comments/1")'>谢郎</span>、也恨飘零，解道月明千里。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_178844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_178844'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(178844)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>岁暮留越，作《玲珑四犯》（叠鼓夜寒）<div id='poem_178876' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178876' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178876?labeling=true' target='_blank'>玲珑四犯 此曲双调，世别有大石调一曲越中岁暮闻箫鼓感怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178876")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178876_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178876'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178876'>叠鼓夜寒，垂灯春浅，匆匆时事如许。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178876_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178876'>倦游欢意少，俛仰悲今古。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178876_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178876'>江淹又吟恨赋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178876_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178876'>记当时、送君南浦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178876_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178876'>万里乾坤，百年身世，唯有此情苦。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178876_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178876'>扬州柳，垂官路。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178876_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178876'>有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_178876", 178876, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>轻盈</span>换马，端正窥户。<div id='poem_sentence_6_178876_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178876'>酒醒明月下，梦逐潮声去。<div id='poem_sentence_7_178876_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_178876'>文章信美知何用，漫赢得、天涯羁旅。<div id='poem_sentence_8_178876_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_178876'>教说与。<div id='poem_sentence_9_178876_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_178876'>春来要、寻花伴侣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_178876_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='f74b9a0413ef4c65b78f70e712b44bca_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f74b9a0413ef4c65b78f70e712b44bca");'><span id='f74b9a0413ef4c65b78f70e712b44bca_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>，39岁</div><div id='f74b9a0413ef4c65b78f70e712b44bca' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>复返越。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>作《寄上郑郎中》诗，当作于此时。作品：寄上郑郎中。<span class='inlineComment2'>（陈思《白石年谱》第2140页。）</span><div id='poem_178715' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178715' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178715?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄上郑郎中</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178715")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_178715_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178715'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178715'>梅根东望九华云，中有风流衣绣人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178715'>名下一生劳梦想，尊前数语倍情亲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178715'>节旄在道催归汉，花鸟留君且作春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178715'>见说祥风挟时雨，故园松菊亦精神。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178715_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178715'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_178715_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='a094ef01bff0421caf996a066daded60_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a094ef01bff0421caf996a066daded60");'><span id='a094ef01bff0421caf996a066daded60_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1201&endYear=1201')">1201年</a>，47岁</div><div id='a094ef01bff0421caf996a066daded60' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，入越，朱鼐赠绛帖。作品：绛帖平自序。<div id='poem_1288459' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1288459' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1288459?labeling=true' target='_blank'>绛帖平序</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉泰三年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_1288459")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1288459_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1288459'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1288459'>小学既废，流为法书，法书又废，唯存法帖，法帖乃古人陈迹耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1288459_comment'></div>况数经摹刻，已失笔意，然苟能习之，亦胜面墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1288459_comment'></div>法帖始自贞观，褚遂良所校馆本《十七帖》是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1288459_comment'></div>我太宗皇帝造《淳化阁帖》十卷，自后有所谓刘丞相沆潭、潘尚书师旦绛、临江刘次庄、宗氏将字、世章汝刻《续帖大观》之类，不可胜计，要皆本诸《淳化帖》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1288459_comment'></div>《淳化帖》今难得，而诸家旧帖亦不易致，《绛帖》传至今者复有三四本，潘师旦所刻为胜，绛公库本次之，厥后漫灭，屡经补治，甚至字画乖讹，尝以相校，乃知其有三四本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1288459_comment'></div>嘉泰辛酉，予入越，友人朱子大以绛帖遗予，归而玩之，因为之本事释文，名曰《绛帖平》。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1288459_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>送陈敬甫诗。<div id='poem_178687' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178687' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178687?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送陈敬甫</a><span class='authorDate'>（1201年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178687")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178687_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178687'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178687'>十年所闻溢吾耳，去年诵君书一纸。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178687'>古人三语得奇士，况此磊落数百字。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178687'>相逢千岩万壑里，有客如君请兄事。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178687'>才高自古人所忌，论高不售反惊世。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178687'>好诗取客如券契，我无三者犹至是。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178687'>如君之贫不可避，如君之贫不可避，呼舟径度寒潮外。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_178687_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>作《徵招》词。（潮回却过西陵浦）<div id='poem_178911' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178911' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178911?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徵招</a><span class='authorDate'>（1201年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178911")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178911_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_178911'>越中山水幽远。予数上下西兴、钱清间，襟抱清旷。越人善为舟，卷篷方底，舟师行歌，徐徐曳之，如偃卧榻上，无动摇突兀势，以故得尽情骋望。予欲家焉而未得，作徵招以寄兴。徵招、角招者，政和间，大晟府尝制数十曲，音节驳矣。予尝考唐田畸声律要诀云：徵与二变之调，咸非流美，故自古少徵调曲也。徵为去母调，如黄钟之徵，以黄钟为线，不用黄钟乃谐。故随唐旧谱，不用母声，琴家无媒调、商调之类。皆徵也，亦皆具母弦而不用。其说详于予所作琴书。然黄钟以林钟为徵，住声于林钟。若不用黄钟声，便自成林钟宫矣。故大晟府徵调兼母声，一句似林钟均，所以当时有落韵之语。予尝使人吹而听之，寄君声于臣民事物之中，清者高而亢，浊者下而遗，万宝常所谓宫离而不附者是已。因再三推寻唐谱并琴弦法而得其意。黄钟徵虽不用母声，亦不可多用变徵蕤宾、变宫庆钟声。若不用黄钟而用蕤宾、应钟，即是林钟宫矣。馀十一均徵调傲此。其法可谓善矣。然无清声，只可施之琴瑟，难入燕乐。故燕乐阙徵调，不必补可也。此一曲乃予昔所制，因旧央正宫齐天乐慢前两拍是徵调，故足成之。虽兼用母声，较大晟曲为无病矣。此曲依晋史名曰黄钟下徵调、角招曰黄钟清角调</div><div id='poem_preface_178911_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178911'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178911'>潮回却过西陵浦，扁舟仅容居士。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178911_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178911'>去得几何时，黍离离如此。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178911_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178911'>客途今倦矣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178911_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178911'>漫赢得、一襟诗思。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178911_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178911'>记忆江南，落帆沙际，此行还是。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178911_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178911'>迤逦。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178911_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178911'>剡中山，重相见、依依故人情味。<div id='poem_sentence_6_178911_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178911'>似怨不来游，拥愁鬟十二。<div id='poem_sentence_7_178911_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_178911'>一丘聊复尔。<div id='poem_sentence_8_178911_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_178911'>也孤负、幼舆高志。<div id='poem_sentence_9_178911_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_178911'>水荭晚，漠漠摇烟，奈未成归计。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_178911_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='58e20384c03c435f8c41b0a304fb69f6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("58e20384c03c435f8c41b0a304fb69f6");'><span id='58e20384c03c435f8c41b0a304fb69f6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1203&endYear=1203')">1203年</a>，49岁</div><div id='58e20384c03c435f8c41b0a304fb69f6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1203&endYear=1203')">1203年</a>　后月余，过钱清，又记其后。<br /></div>
-----end

德清

-----title
吴淞街道
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1ee8bde2b57748b2a82f0e8e5131b90f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1ee8bde2b57748b2a82f0e8e5131b90f");'><span id='1ee8bde2b57748b2a82f0e8e5131b90f_link'
