href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年</a>　道经吴淞，作《庆宫春》。过旬涂稿乃定。（双桨蓴波）<div id='poem_178855' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178855' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178855?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庆宫春</a><span class='authorDate'>（1196年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178855")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178855_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_178855'>绍熙辛亥除夕，予别石湖归吴兴，雪后夜过垂虹，尝赋诗云：“笠泽茫茫雁影微。玉峰重垒护云衣。长桥寂寞春寒夜，只有诗人一舸归。”后五年冬，复与俞商卿、张平甫、铦朴翁自封禺同载诣梁溪，道经吴松。山寒天迥，云浪四合。中夕相呼步垂虹，星斗下垂，错杂渔火，朔吹凛凛，卮酒不能支。朴翁以衾自缠，犹相与行吟，因赋此阕，盖过旬涂稿乃定。朴翁咎予无益，然意所耽，不能自己也。平甫，商卿，朴翁皆工于诗，所出奇诡，予亦强追逐之。此行既归，各得五十馀解</div><div id='poem_preface_178855_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178855'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178855'>双桨莼波，一蓑松雨，暮愁渐满<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_178855", 178855, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>空阔</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178855'>呼我盟鸥，翩翩欲下，背人还过木末。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178855'>那回归去，荡云雪、孤舟夜发。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178855'>伤心重见，依约眉山，黛痕低压。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178855_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178855'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_178855", 178855, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>采香径</span>里春寒，老子婆娑，自歌谁答。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178855'>垂虹西望，飘然引去，此兴平生难遏。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
无锡
-----detail

id='poem_sentence_3_178883'>书寄岭头封不到，影浮杯面误人吹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178883'>寂寥惟有夜寒知。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_178883_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_178884' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178884' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178884?labeling=true' target='_blank'>浣溪沙<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1196年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178884")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178884_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178884'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178884'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_178884", 178884, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>剪剪</span>寒花小更垂。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178884_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178884'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_178884", 178884, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>阿琼</span>愁里弄妆迟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178884_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178884'>东风烧烛夜深归。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178884_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178884'>落蕊半黏钗上燕，露横斜映鬓边犀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178884_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178884'>老夫无味已多时。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_178884_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
桐庐
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6a60e50307ee41d0b58f593af76cb78e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6a60e50307ee41d0b58f593af76cb78e");'><span id='6a60e50307ee41d0b58f593af76cb78e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1206&endYear=1206')">1206年</a>，52岁</div><div id='6a60e50307ee41d0b58f593af76cb78e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1206&endYear=1206')">1206年</a>　南游浙东，过桐庐，登乌石寺，有诗。<div id='poem_178765' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178765' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178765?labeling=true' target='_blank'>登乌石寺观张魏公刘安成岳武穆留题刘云侍儿意真奉命题记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1206年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178765")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_178765_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178765'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178765'>诸老凋零极可哀，尚留名字压崔嵬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178765_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178765'>刘郎可是疏文墨，几点胭脂污绿苔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178765_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178765'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_178765_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
丽水
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e461399e51cf42ecaaf37d6de7685ce4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e461399e51cf42ecaaf37d6de7685ce4");'><span id='e461399e51cf42ecaaf37d6de7685ce4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1206&endYear=1206')">1206年</a>，52岁</div><div id='e461399e51cf42ecaaf37d6de7685ce4' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋至括苍，登烟雨楼，作《虞美人》词。（阑干表立苍龙背）<div id='poem_178906' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178906' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178906?labeling=true' target='_blank'>虞美人</a><span class='authorDate'>（1206年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178906")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178906_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_178906'>括苍烟雨楼，石湖居士所造也。风景似越之蓬莱阁，而山势环绕，峰岭高秀过之，观居士题颜，且歌其所虞美人。羲亦作一解</div><div id='poem_preface_178906_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178906'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178906'>阑干表立苍龙背。三面搀天翠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178906_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178906'>东游才上小蓬莱。不见此楼烟雨、未应回。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178906_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178906'>而今<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_178906", 178906, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>指点</span>来时路。却是冥濛处。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178906_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178906'>老仙鹤驭几时归。未必山川城郭、是耶非。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178906_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178906'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_178906_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>与处州太守赵癰东堂联句。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
温州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5a6b3efaa0ec48579c2639300876b814_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5a6b3efaa0ec48579c2639300876b814");'><span id='5a6b3efaa0ec48579c2639300876b814_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1206&endYear=1206')">1206年</a>，52岁</div><div id='5a6b3efaa0ec48579c2639300876b814' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1206&endYear=1206')">1206年</a>　抵永嘉，游富览亭，作《水调歌头》（日落爱山紫）<div id='poem_178845' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_178845' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/178845?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头 富览亭永嘉作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1206年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25195, "南宋", "姜夔", "poem_title_178845")'>姜夔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_178845_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_178845'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_178845'>日落爱山紫，沙涨省潮回。<div id='poem_sentence_0_178845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_178845'>平生梦犹不到，一叶眇西来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_178845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_178845'>欲讯桑田成海，人世了无知者，鱼鸟两相猜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_178845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_178845'>天外玉笙杳，子晋只空台。<div id='poem_sentence_3_178845_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_178845'>倚阑干，二三子，总仙才。<div id='poem_sentence_4_178845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_178845'>尔歌远游章句，云气入吾杯。<div id='poem_sentence_5_178845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_178845'>不问王郎五马，颇忆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_178845", 178845, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>谢生</span>双屐，处处长青苔。<div id='poem_sentence_6_178845_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_178845'>东望赤城近，吾兴亦悠哉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_178845_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
